SkP iti skandapurāṇe nāma trayodaśo dhyāyaḥSkandapurana sanatkumāra uvācaatha vṛtte vivāhe tu bhavasyāmitatejasaḥ praharṣamatulaṃ gatvā devāḥ sahapitāmahāḥ tuṣṭuvurvāgbhiriṣṭābhiḥ praṇamanto  SkP tato sya netrajo vahnir jvālāmālāsahasravān saṃvṛtya ratibhartāram adahatsaparicchadam  SkP sa dahyamānaḥ karuṇam ārto krośata visvaram prasādayaṃśca taṃ devaṃ papāta sa mahītale  SkP āśu so gniparītāṅgo manmatho lokatāpanaḥ papāta bhasmasāccaiva kṣaṇena samapadyata  SkP patnī tu karuṇaṃ tasya vilalāpa suduḥkhitā devaṃ devīṃ ca duḥkhārtā ayācatkaruṇāyatī  SkP tasyāśca karuṇāṃ śrutvā devau vasiṣṭhasya ca tāṃ kṣāntiṃ jñātvā sa ṛṣipuṃgavaḥ  SkP viśvāmitro mahātejā vasiṣṭhe vairamatyajat evaṃ tau vairamanyonyaṃ jahaturmunisattamau  SkP sanatkumāra uvācaya imaṃ śṛṇuyānnityaṃ brāhmaṇāñchrāvayīta vā sa dustarāṇi durgāṇi taratyaśrāntapauruṣaḥ  SkP hrīpauruṣaudāryavihārasattvaiḥ samanvitaḥ sojjvalacāruveṣaḥ bhavecca sarvāmararājatulyas tripiṣṭape krīḍati cecchayā svayam  SkP evaṃ tadabhavadvyāsa viśvāmitravasiṣṭhayoḥ vairaṃ samāptaṃ lokānāṃ hitārthaṃ punareva ca  SkP iti skandapurāṇe ūnaviṃśatitamo dhyāyaḥSkandapurana vyāsa uvācaumāharau tu deveśau cakraturyacca saṃgatau tanme sarvamaśeṣeṇa kathayasva mahāmune  SkP sanatkumāra uvācaumāharau tu saṃgamya parasparamaninditau śālaṅkasyānvaye vipraṃ yuyujāte vareṇa ha  SkP sa cāpyayonijaḥ putra ārādhya parameśvaram rudreṇa samatāṃ labdhvā mahāgaṇapatirbabhau  SkP vyāsa uvācakathaṃ nandī samutpannaḥ kathaṃ cārādhya śaṃkaram samānatvamagācchambhoḥ pratīhāratvameva ca  SkP sanatkumāra uvācaabhūdṛṣiḥ sa dharmātmā śilādo nāma vīryavān tasyābhūcchilakairvṛttiḥ śilādastena so bhavat  SkP apaśyallambamānāṃstu gartāyāṃ sa pitṝndvijaḥ vicchinnasaṃtatīnghoraṃ nirayaṃ vai prapetuṣaḥ  SkP tairukto patyakāmaistu devaṃ lokeśamavyayam ārādhaya mahādevaṃ sutārthaṃ dvijasattama  SkP tasya varṣasahasreṇa tapyamānasya śūladhṛk śarvaḥ somo gaṇavṛto varado smītyabhāṣata  SkP taṃ dṛṣṭvā somamīśeśaṃ praṇataḥ pādayorvibhoḥ harṣagadgadayā vācā tuṣṭāva vibudheśvaram  SkP namaḥ paramadevāya maheśāya mahātmane sraṣṭre sarvasureśānāṃ brahmaṇaḥ pataye namaḥ  SkP namaḥ kāmāṅganāśāya yogasambhavahetave namaḥ parvatavāsāya dhyānagamyāya vedhase  SkP ṛṣīṇāṃ pataye nityaṃ devānāṃ pataye namaḥ vedānāṃ pataye caiva yogināṃ pataye namaḥ  SkP pradhānāya namo nityaṃ tattvāyāmarasaṃjñiṇe varadāya ca bhaktānāṃ namaḥ sarvagatāya ca  SkP tanmātrendriyabhūtānāṃ vikārāṇāṃ guṇaiḥ saha sraṣṭre ca pataye caiva namaśca prabhaviṣṇave  SkP jagataḥ pataye caiva jagatsraṣṭre namaḥ sadā prakṛteḥ pataye nityaṃ puruṣātparagāmine  SkP īśvarāya namo nityaṃ yogagamyāya raṃhase saṃsārotpattināśāya sarvakāmapradāya ca  SkP śaraṇyāya namo nityaṃ namo bhasmāṅgarāgiṇe namaste yograhastāya tejasāṃ pataye namaḥ  SkP sūryānilahutāśāmbu candrākāśadharāya ca sthitāya sarvadā nityaṃ namastrailokavedhase  SkP stotavyasya kuto deva viśrāmastava vidyate yadā hetustvamevāsya jagataḥ sthitināśayoḥ  SkP aśaraṇyasya deveśa tvattaśca śaraṇārthinaḥ prasādaṃ paramālambya varado bhava viśvakṛt  SkP sanatkumāra uvācayaḥ stotrametadakhilaṃ paṭhate dvijanmā prātaḥ śucirniyamavānpurato dvijānām taṃ brahmarākṣasaniśācarabhūtayakṣā sajjamānayā  SkP bhagavanyadi tuṣṭo si yadi deyo varaśca me icchāmyātmasamaṃ putraṃ mṛtyuhīnamayonijam  SkP evamuktastato devaḥ prīyamāṇastrilocanaḥ evamastviti taṃ procya tatraivāntaradhīyata  SkP gate tasminmaheṣvāse ṛṣiḥ paramapūjitaḥ svamāśramamupāgamya ṛṣibhyo kathayattataḥ  SkP taiḥ praśastastataścaiva kālena munisattama yiyakṣuryajñabhūmiṃ svāṃ lāṅgalena cakarṣa tām  SkP tasyāṃ tu kṛṣyamāṇāyāṃ sītāyāṃ tatsamutthitaḥ saṃvartakānalaprakhyaḥ kumāraḥ pratyadṛśyata  SkP sa taṃ dṛṣṭvā tathodbhūtaṃ kumāraṃ dīptatejasam rākṣaso yamiti jñātvā bhayānnopasasāra tam  SkP kumāro pi tathodbhūtaḥ pitaraṃ dīptatejasam upāsarpata dīnātmā tāta tāteti cābravīt  SkP sa tātetyucyamāno pi yadā taṃ nābhyanandata tato vāyustamākāśe śilādaṃ prāha susvaram  SkP vāyuruvācaśālaṅkāyana putraste yo sau devena śambhunā ayonijaḥ purā dattaḥ sa eṣa pratinandaya  SkP yasmānnandīkaraste yaṃ sadaiva dvijasattama tasmānnandīti nāmnāyaṃ bhaviṣyati sutastava  SkP sanatkumāra uvācatataḥ sa vāyuvacanān nandinaṃ pariṣasvaje gṛhītvā cāśramaṃ svena so nayattuṣṭivardhanam cūḍopanayanādīni karmāṇyasya cakāra saḥ  SkP kṛtvā cādhyāpayāmāsa vedānsāṅgānaśeṣataḥ āyurvedaṃ dhanurvedaṃ gāndharvaṃ śabdalakṣaṇam  SkP hastināṃ caritaṃ yacca naranāryośca lakṣaṇam śilpāni caiva sarvāṇi nimittajñānameva ca  SkP bhūtagrāmacikitsāṃ ca mātṝṇāṃ caritaṃ ca yat bhujaṃgānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ yacca kiṃcidviceṣṭitam abdairadhītavānsarvaṃ vyāsa pañcabhireva ca  SkP dakṣaḥ śuciradīnātmā priyavāganasūyakaḥ sarvalokapriyo nityaṃ manonayananandanaḥ  SkP tasyātha saptame varṣe ṛṣī divyau tapodhanau āśramaṃ kṛcchramāviśat  SkP nandyuvācasatyaṃ devaṛṣī tāta na tāvanṛtamūcatuḥ tathāpi tu na mṛtyurme prabhaviṣyati mā śucaḥ  SkP śilāda uvācakiṃ tapaḥ kiṃ parijñānaṃ ko yogaḥ kaḥ śramaśca te yena tvaṃ SkP japatā tena tatraiva tatpareṇa tadāśiṣā koṭirekā yadā japtā tadā devastutoṣa ha  SkP tamāgatyāha bhagavāñ charva ugraḥ kapardimān nandiṃstuṣṭo smi bhadraṃ te varaṃ vṛṇu yathepsitam  SkP uvāca devadeveśo bhaktyā paramayā yutam aśrupūrṇekṣaṇaṃ dīnaṃ pādayoḥ śirasā natam  SkP karābhyāṃ susukhābhyāṃ tu saṃgṛhya paramārtihā utthāpya nayane somaḥ aśrupūrṇe mamārja ha  SkP uvāca cainaṃ tuṣṭātmā vacasāpyāyayanniva nirīkṣya gaṇapānsarvān devyā saha tadā prabhuḥ  SkP deva uvācajāne bhaktiṃ tava mayi jāne cārtiṃ tavānagha tasya sarvasya śailāde udarkaṃ saṃniśāmaya  SkP amaro jarayā tyakto nityaṃ duḥkhavivarjitaḥ akṣayaścāvyayaścaiva sapitā sasuhṛjjanaḥ  SkP mameṣṭo gaṇapaścaiva madvīryo matparākramaḥ iṣṭo mama sadā caiva mama pārśvagataḥ sadā madrūpaścaiva bhavitā mahāyogabalānvitaḥ  SkP ṛddhimaccaiva te dvīpaṃ kṣīrodamamṛtākaram saṃvāsaṃ samprayacchāmi tatra raṃsyasi sarvadā  SkP kuśeśayamayīṃ mālām avamucyātmanastataḥ ābabandha mahātejā nandine divyarūpiṇīm  SkP sa tayā mālayā nandī babhau kaṇṭhāvasaktayā tryakṣo daśabhujaḥ śrīmān dvitīya iva śaṃkaraḥ  SkP tatastaṃ vai samādāya hastena bhagavānharaḥ uvāca brūhi kiṃ te dya dadāni varamuttamam  SkP āśramaścāyamatyarthaṃ tapasā tava bhāvitaḥ japyeśvara iti khyāto mama guhyo bhaviṣyati  SkP samantādyojanaṃ kṣetraṃ divyaṃ devagaṇairvṛtam siddhacāraṇasaṃkīrṇam apsarogaṇasevitam siddhikṣetraṃ paraṃ guhyaṃ bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ  SkP karmaṇā manasā vācā yatkiṃcitkurute naraḥ śubhaṃ vāpyaśubhaṃ vātra sarvaṃ bhavitṛ tacchubham  SkP jāpyaṃ mānasaṃ tulyaṃ vai rudrāṇāṃ tadbhaviṣyati yatra tatra mṛtā martyā yāsyanti tava lokatām  SkP tato jaṭāsrutaṃ vāri gṛhītvā hāranirmalam uktvā nadī bhavasveti visasarja mahātapāḥ  SkP sā tato divyatoyā ca puṇyā maṇijalā śubhā haṃsakāraṇḍavākīrṇā cakravākopaśobhitā padmotpalavanopetā prāvartata tebhyastathābhyupetebhyo nikumbhaḥ sa mahāyaśāḥ dadau sarvānabhiprāyān ye ye teṣāmabhīpsitāḥ  SkP evaṃ taṃ kāmadaṃ jñātvā divodāso nṛpastadā uvāca mahiṣīṃ vyāsa kadācitputralipsayā  SkP devi sarvānabhiprāyāñ janebhyo yaṃ prayacchati gaṇeśvaraṃ tvamapyenam apatyārthaṃ prasādaya  SkP saivamuktā tadā gatvā gaṇeśaṃ prāpya śobhanā uvāca bhagavandeva anapatyāhamīśvara  SkP upavāsaṃ kariṣyāmi tava devābhirādhane tāvanna bhokṣye yāvanme varo dattastvayā prabho  SkP jāte ca putre dāsyāmi śatānāṃ daśatīrdaśa tvāmuddiśya dvijātibhyo godhenūnāṃ gaṇeśvara  SkP tathā ghaṭasahasreṇa dadhnaścaiva ghṛtasya ca kṣīrasya pañcagavyasya kariṣye snapanaṃ ca te  SkP brāhmaṇānāṃ sahasrāṇāṃ śataṃ cāpi supūjitam purastādbhojayiṣye te putre jāte na saṃśayaḥ  SkP bahūndāsyati rājā ca grāmāndāsyastathaiva ca sadā sattraṃ ca pūjāṃ ca kariṣyati tava prabho  SkP sanatkumāra uvācasā tamuktvā tathā vyāsa tasthau niyamamāsthitā sopavāsā tadā pūjāṃ mahatīṃ tasya kurvatī  SkP tāṃ tathā tiṣṭhatīṃ devaḥ provāca sa gaṇeśvaraḥ uttiṣṭha nāsti te putro mā khedaṃ tvaṃ vṛthā kṛthāḥ  SkP evaṃ tena gaṇeśena nikumbhena mahātmanā asakṛtprocyamānā sā niyamādvirarāma ha  SkP tato narādhipaṃ devī provāca vimanā tadā āryaputra na me putraṃ gaṇapo sau prayacchati bravīti nāsti te putro mā vṛthā niyamaṃ kṛthāḥ  SkP sanatkumāra uvācaevaṃ mahiṣyā sa proktaḥ svayameva narādhipaḥ sadā saniyamastasthau gaṇeśasyāgrato nṛpaḥ  SkP tamapyuvāca nṛpatiṃ nikumbho niyamasthitam mā sthā vṛtheha nṛpate na te putraṃ dadāmyaham  SkP evamuktaḥ sa rājendro nikumbhena mahābalaḥ krodharaktekṣaṇaḥ prāha tamutthāya gaṇeśvaram  SkP rājovācagaṇo vā tvaṃ piśāco vā bhūto vā rākṣaso pi vā kṛtaghnastvaṃ na saṃdeho na tvaṃ pūjāmihārhasi  SkP mama caiva gṛhadvāri pauraiścaiva samarcitaḥ viṣaye mama vāsī ca na ca putraṃ prayacchasi  SkP pūjārho na bhavāṃstasmān matto daṇḍaṃ tvamarhasi nṛśaṃsaścāvaliptaśca niṣṭhuro matsarānvitaḥ  SkP tato sya bhedayāmāsa nilayaṃ gajayūthapaiḥ sthaṇḍilaṃ ca babhañjāśu dadāhārcāṃ ca suprabhām  SkP nikumbho pi kṛtārthaḥ sann ākāśe saṃsthitaḥ prabhuḥ uvāca taṃ divodāsaṃ pradahanniva tejasā  SkP yatheṣṭaṃ samprayacchanti devā varamabhīpsitam na datto yadyasau kopaḥ kastatra bhavato bhavat  SkP yasmānmamālayo bhagnas tvayā nirapakāriṇaḥ tasmādvarṣasahasraṃ te purī śūnyā bhaviṣyati  SkP sanatkumāra uvācasa evamuktvā rājānaṃ nikumbhaḥ paramātmavān deveśāya nivedyaivaṃ tasthau pārśvagataḥ prabhoḥ  SkP rājāpi tasya vākyena tathyenārthena caiva hi vrīḍāṃ parāṃ samāsādya gṛhānabhyāgamattadā  SkP atha sā tena śāpena purī vārāṇasī tadā śūnyā samabhavatkṣipraṃ viśuddhā mṛgasevitā  SkP tāṃ tu śūnyāṃ sa vijñāya devyā saha pinākadhṛk sagaṇo nandinā sārdham ājagāma mahādyutiḥ  SkP sa tatra mānasaṃ divyaṃ vimānaṃ sūryavarcasam anaupamyaguṇaṃ devo manasaivābhinirmime  SkP na me prabhavati śubhāśubham  SkP vyāsa uvācakiṃ tatsa bhagavāndevaḥ prīyamāṇo mahātapāḥ praṇayātsa tadā devyā pṛṣṭo kathayadavyayaḥ  SkP sanatkumāra uvācamayāpyetatpurā vyāsa pṛṣṭo nandīśvaraḥ prabhuḥ yathoktavānmayi kautūhalaṃ hi me  SkP nandīśvara uvācaśrūyatāmabhidhāsyāmi pṛcchataste mahāmune devadevena pārvatyā yatpurā kathitaṃ hitam  SkP deva uvācaśrūyatāmabhidhāsyāmi yanmāṃ pṛcchasi suvrate hitāya devi sārdhaṃ nityamaṣṭaguṇānvitaḥ  SkP kāñcanaṃ tuṭimātraṃ vā yo dadyādbahu vā mama tasya haimavate śṛṅge dadāni gṛhamuttamam  SkP yo me gāstu hiraṇyaṃ vā dadyādavimanāḥ priye lokāndadānyahaṃ tasmai mahimānopacāraiśca yo māṃ japyaiśca pūjayet dadāni brahmaṇo loke vāsaṃ tasya supūjitam  SkP manasā cintayedyaśca pūjayeyamahaṃ haram aśakto nāsti ca dravyaṃ yasya nityaṃ sumadhyame  SkP sa tayā sarvathā vartamāno pi devi yo māṃ sadā smaret kalmaṣeṇa na yujyeta naraḥ kartā kadācana  SkP sarvāvastho pi pāpātmā jñānaniṣṭhena cetasā yo bhyarcayati māṃ nityaṃ sa mamātmasamo bhavet  SkP ṣaḍaṅgena śarva bhīma paśupate śaṃkarogra bhaveti ca mahādeveti cāpyanyan nāma guhyaṃ prakīrtayet sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyeta divi devaiśca pūjyate  SkP eteṣāmekamapi yaḥ kathayedvā paṭheta vā sa dehapaddhatiṃ bhittvā māmeva pratipadyate evaṃ sarvapraṇāmena yanmayā parikīrtitam  SkP amāvāsyāṃ tu yo nityaṃ saghṛtaṃ gugguluṃ dahet kṣīreṇa caiva saṃmiśraṃ guhyametanmama priye so cyutaṃ sthānamāpnoti matprasādānna saṃśayaḥ  SkP idaṃ ca paramaṃ guhyaṃ yo me devi nivedayet arkaparṇapuṭaṃ pūrṇaṃ ghṛtasya madhunā saha nivedya vidhivadbhaktyā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate  SkP imāni ca mahābhāge yo me nāmāni kīrtayet śmaśānanilayo nagno bhasmaśāyī yatavrataḥ  SkP vāmadevaḥ praśāntaśca stabdhaśephastrilocanaḥ avasavyapriyaḥ savyo bahurūpo ntakāntakṛt  SkP purāṇaḥ puruhūtaśca mṛtyormṛtyurjitendriyaḥ viśrutaḥ  SkP yaścemaṃ tvatkṛtaṃ liṅgaṃ niyamenārcayiṣyati yonayaḥ sapta gatvā tu yogaṃ sa samavāpsyati  SkP jaigīṣavyaguhāṃ cemāṃ prāpya yo yokṣyate dvijaḥ sa saptarātraṃ yuktātmā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate  SkP māsena pūrvāṃ jātiṃ ca pūrvādhītaṃ ca vetsyati ekarātraṃ gatiṃ śuddhāṃ dvābhyāṃ tārayate pitṝn  SkP trirātreṇa vyatītāṃśca parānsapta ca tārayet ato bhūyaśca kiṃ te dya jaigīṣavya dadānyaham  SkP jaigīṣavya uvācabhagavandevadeveśa yaccha yanme manogatam ato haṃ nānyadicchāmi yogākṣayyātparaṃ hitam  SkP tvayi bhaktiśca nityaṃ syāt some sagaṇapeśvare anutsekaṃ tathā kṣāntiṃ śamaṃ damamathāpi ca  SkP na cāpyabhibhavaṃ kuryān na ca tejovamānanām etānvarānahaṃ deva sadecchāmi mahādyute  SkP deva uvācaete tava bhaviṣyanti ajayyatvaṃ ca yogibhiḥ icchato darśanaṃ caiva bhaviṣyati ca te mama  SkP sanatkumāra uvācatataḥ sa bhagavāndevaḥ pārāśaryomayā saha sanandī sagaṇaścaiva bhaktānugrahalipsayā  SkP tapyato yakṣarājasya kṛtvā hṛdi maheśvaram varadānāya deveśo jagāma puratastadā
